foreword

In book written aforetim set forth
print therein told much histori king arthur
manifest royalti achiev wonder magic sword
drew forth anvil establish royalti
found splendid sword yclept excalibur miracul wonder
manner beauti ladi world queen
establish famou round tabl nobl worthi knight
like whose prowess world hath never seen like
ever behold

also told book adventur certain worthi knight
likewis magician merlin betray undo sorceress
hight vivien

now took joy read book great hope
follow may everi whit pleas shall hereinaft
adventur certain worthi may
alreadi becom acquaint book otherwis likewis
adventur certain worthi yet
told

more especi believ find entertain shall
tell adventur great knight altogeth
nobl spirit beauti bravest heart
knight ever live except son galahad
crown glori hous name reign king
arthur

howev sir launcelot lake fail behavior
world shall say never fell error and
offend shall hardihood say never
commit offenc

yea maketh launcelot singularli dear world
differ men like men
virtu shortcom strong brave
untir us brethren
endeavor failur

prologu

It hath alreadi set forth print volum written
concern adventur king arthur first becam king
certain lesser king favor friendli alli
certain other sort
enemi

among friend king ban benwick
exceedingli nobl lord high estat great honor
lineag exalt like anyon world
higher strain

sidenot Of king ban misfortun now upon certain time king
ban benwick fell great troubl came
power enemi wit king clauda scotland king clauda brought unto
benwick huge armi knight lord sat
castl tribl intent take strong fortress destroy

thi nobl castl tribl chiefest strongest place
defenc king ban dominion wherefor intrench
knight queen hight helen
youngest son hight launcelot

now child launcelot dearer queen helen world
besid larg limb extraordinarili beauti
face believ angel paradis could
beauti He born singular birthmark upon
shoulder birthmark appear golden star enstamp
upon skin wherefor queen would say launcelot
reason star upon thi shoulder believ thou shalt
star hous thou shalt shine remark glori
world shall behold thi lustr shall marvel thereat time
come So queen took extraordinari delight launcelot love
core heart albeit knew time
spake propheci concern star fall
perfectli true

now though king ban thought well defend castl
tribl yet king clauda brought terribl big armi place
cover entir plain great mani battl fought
wall castl ever king clauda wax greater stronger
king ban parti grew weaker fear

sidenot king ban bethink king arthur So thing came
pass king ban bethought king arthur said
go lord king beseech help aid
certainli give nor trust messeng
affair go king arthur
speak lip

have thu bethought sent queen helen come privi
closet said My dear love noth remaineth
go unto court king arthur beseech lend power aid
extrem misfortun trust messeng
affair now castl place thee
away therefor go upon busi take thee
launcelot leav safeti king arthur
court son sir ector war end done and
queen helen lent assent

So king ban summon senesch castl name sir
malydor le brun said messir go henc tonight secret
pass intent betak unto king arthur beseech aid
extrem moreov shall take ladi young child
launcelot place within care king arthur
dolor war but besid take one
favorit esquir foliot now charg thee sir hold castl
behalf thi might main yield enemi upon
extrem believ shall littl return
suffici aid king arthur compass relief place

sidenot king ban queen helen launcelot escap tribl So
night fallen dark still king ban queen helen
young child launcelot esquir foliot left town privili
mean postern gate thenc went secret path known
led steep decliv rock wall rock upon
either side high inde came safeti
beyond armi king clauda forest valley
and forest lay still solemn dark silenc
nighttim

have thu come safeti forest small parti journey
celer abl achiev littl time
dawn came lake water open meadow
forest here rest littl queen helen fallen
weari rough hasti journey travel

sidenot foliot seeth light now whilst sat rest foliot
spake sudden say unto king ban lord light
maketh sky bright yonderway then king ban look littl
present said methink must dawn break lord
quoth foliot well light sky lieth
south whenc come east sun
aris

then king ban heart misgav soul shaken great
troubl foliot said believ speak sooth
light bode ill us then said stay littl
go discov light may therewith mount
hors rode away dark

sidenot king ban beholdeth burn tribl now
high hill nearbi upon top hill open
platform rock whenc man could see great way everi direct
So king ban went place come cast
eye direct light straightway beheld manner
terror light came tribl terror still
grow greater heart beheld town castl
one great flame fire

when king ban saw sat upon hors like one turn
stone then cri great voic woe
woe woe and cri still loud voic cert
god hath desert entir

sidenot the death king ban therewith great passion grief took
hold upon shook like leaf immedi
felt someth brake within sharp bitter pain
wist heart broken So alon
upon hilltop perfect still night cri
My heart My heart and therewith shadow death come upon
could sit longer upon hors fell upon ground
and knew well death nigh cross pray
upon took two blade grass twist holi sign
kiss pray unto god would forgiv sin So
die alon upon hilltop

meanwhil queen helen foliot sat togeth wait return
present heard sound hors hoof come
rocki path then queen helen said foliot methink lord cometh So
littl came hors empti saddl when foliot beheld
said ladi meseem great troubl come us methink
someth hath befallen lord sore travail
hors without

then seem queen helen though spirit life suddenli went
away foresaw befallen So aros like one
dream speak quietli said foliot take whither
lord went awhil sinc To foliot said ladi wait
morn near hand dark go
thitherward present whereunto ladi helen repli foliot
wait stay wait believ shall go mad upon
foliot tri persuad made readi take
whither would go

now young child launcelot asleep upon queen knee
wherefor took cloak wrap child laid
gentli upon ground wake then mount upon
palfrey foliot led palfrey hill whither king ban gone
short time sinc

sidenot the ladi helen findeth king when came place
open rock told found king ban lie quiet still
upon ground counten great peac for believ
sureti god forgiven sin would suffer
care troubl life thu queen helen
found find made moan outcri kind
look long dead face could see
plainli dawn alreadi broken and
said dear lord thou art time happier case and
said foliot Go bring hors place
may bear henc ladi said foliot good
left alon foliot said queen thou dost know much
alon thi leav make alon therewith
fell weep great passion

then foliot wept also great measur still weep like rain
went away left when came king ban hors sun
risen bird sing great jubil
everyth blith gay one could believ care
troubl could dwell world beauti

sidenot the ladi helen bringeth dead mountain So
queen helen foliot lift dead king hors queen
said come thou foliot thine gait go ahead seek
child yet launcelot joy hapli need
moment So queen made hast steep hill ahead
foliot came margin littl lake
rest awhil sinc

By sun risen strong warm lake
meadow circumadjac forest stood around meadow
illumin glori effulg

now queen helen enter meadow beheld wonder
ladi ladi bare child launcelot arm and
ladi sang launcelot young child look face
laugh set hand cheek all queen helen beheld
likewis beheld ladi extraordinari
appear clad altogeth green glister shone
wonder bright and beheld around neck ladi
necklac gold inset opal stone emerald perceiv

ladi wonder beauti behold look
upon felt manner fear ladi fay

and ladi ladi lake spoken aforetim book
king arthur wherein told aid king arthur obtain
wonder famou sword yclept excalibur aid sir pellia
gentl knight time extrem took lake
also diver thing concern told therein

then queen came near ladi said

ladi pray give child upon ladi lake
smile strang said thou shalt thi child ladi
littl thou shalt then queen helen cri
great agoni passion ladi would take child
give left world Lo
lost hous land husband joy life
give wherefor beseech take child To

ordain must take thi child take may
give thee rear wise shall make glori
thi hous glori world for shall becom greatest
knight world loin shall spring greater still

child give

sidenot the ladi lake taketh launcelot lake therewith
would laid hold garment ladi lake
supplic ladi lake drew away queen helen

vanish face mirror

for breath upon mirror breath obscur lieth

then queen helen fell swoon lay besid lake

like death knew whether dead So
knew sat made great lament long


sidenot the ladi helen taketh nunneri what time sat thu
came way three nun dwelt abbey nun

sidenot how launcelot dwelt lake now launcelot dwelt nigh
seventeen year ladi nymu lake wonder
beauti valley cover appear magic lake
hath aforetim describ book king arthur

and land lake sort shall describ

unto anyon could enter magic water lake
mortal allow come
meadow faeri conceal beneath enchant water
would behold wide radiant field extraordinari
beauti and would behold field cover
multitud exquisit beauti flower heart
behold would elat pure joy find midst
wave sea multitudin fragrant blossom and would behold mani
fair shadi grove tree grew

and would perhap behold pleasant place beneath shade
tree parti fair gentl folk countri

such land unto launcelot brought
told may see wonder beauti place

and mysteri place enter soul launcelot

fellowmort dwelt

for though smile great deal often laugh
laugh never scorn alway lovingkind



It land sir pellia dwelt sever year

chapter first


how sir launcelot came forth from enchant castl lake
enter into world again how king arthur made him knight

sidenot Of springtim long ago know time year
full joy earli summer season time
sun wonder lusti strong yet hot time
tree shrub full life abund shade yet
grown dri heat drought later day time
grass young lush green walk athwart
meadowland though walk fair billowi lake
magic verdur sprinkl great multitud littl flower
time rose everywher abloom white rose
red eglantin abund time nest brim
wellfledg nestl littl heart small parent fowl
exalt glad sing might
main earli daytim fill full sweet jargon
jubil medley voic yea goodli season year
though hapli spirit may hilari young
golden springtim yet doth soul take great content
ful beauti world heart elat
great abund joy apt feel anoth season

sidenot king arthur two knight ride ahunt now chanc upon
day saint john day ful summertim
king arthur look forth chamber earli
morn beheld exceedingli fair lusti world
outofdoor fresh young daylight for sun
yet risen though rise sky like pure
gold bright grass leav flower drench
sweet fragrant dew bird sing vehement
heart man could rejoic ful life lay
around

there two knight king arthur time one sir ewain
son morgana le fay king arthur nephew
sir ector de mari son king ban benwick queen
helen latter nobl youth knight youngest
knight round tabl time elect these stood
king arthur look forth window also
took joy sweet summer season unto
king arthur spake say messir meseem fair day
stay within door for cert shame king
prison within mine castl whilst ploughman may free
wold green wood bright sun blue sky
wind blow hill dale now would fain go forth
door enjoy thing wherefor ordain shall go
ahunt day ye shall start other
lord ladi dwell herein awak So let us take hors
hound let us take certain forest huntsmen let us
go forth ahunt green forest day shall holiday
shall leav care behind us shall
disport pleasant place

So king arthur bade made man readi
hand bade huntsmen forest attend thereupon
king ordain then rode forth castl
wide world lay beyond yet earli morn
none castl folk astir know departur

all day hunt forest much joy great sport
turn face toward home day far
spent sun sunk behind top tall leafi tree then
time king arthur gave command bend way
toward camelot

sidenot king arthur companion find strang damsel
dwarf now time eve saint john fairi folk
fay come forth well known world
dwell apart time So king arthur two knight
sever forest huntsmen came certain outli part
forest suddenli awar damsel dwarf wait
road upon travel cross anoth road
perceiv remark appear damsel
like fay for dwarf sat upon milkwhit hors
strang still close shrine hedg hawthorn
damsel wonder fair face marvel
behold moreov clad white samit top toe
garment embroid silver trap garnitur
hors white samit stud bright silver boss
wherefor silver glister sudden lustr
whensoev move littl when king arthur two knight
drew nigh damsel much marvel appear
hail voic high clear cri welcom king
arthur welcom king arthur welcom king arthur say three word
three time welcom sir ewain welcom sir ector de mari
address lord name

damsel quoth king arthur singular know
know now tell us name
whenc come whither go for sureti believ
fay

lord said damsel matter save
court wonder ladi good friend she hath sent
meet beseech come whither shall lead
shall lead unto

damsel said king arthur shall right glad go
desir So lead ladi knight
gladli follow thitherway pay court unto

sidenot king arthur knight follow damsel upon
damsel wave hand draw bridlerein led way
accompani dwarf king arthur two knight follow
parti forest huntsmen hound beagl
follow

By time sun set moon risen fair round
yellow gold make great light silent treetop
everyth embalm twilight world
enshroud mysteri midsumm eve yet though sun gone
light wonder bright wherefor eye could see
stood sharpcut clear vision

So damsel dwarf led way somewhat distanc though
far came sudden open
meadow forest hedg around tree woodland and
king knight awar great bustl mani peopl
work busili set sever pavilion white samit
other prepar tabl feast other upon busi
other upon variou sumptermul packhors
palfrey though belong parti consider
estat

then king arthur beheld distanc
away upon side meadow three peopl sit
crabappl tree upon couch especi prepar
awar peopl chief compani

sidenot king arthur companion brought speak strang
folk the first parti three knight haughti nobl
appear clad armor white silver jupon white
embroid silver scabbard sword swordbelt
white shield hung crabtre
white silver thi knight still wore helmet
counten seen the second parti three ladi
clad white raiment her face cover wimpl
counten also seen clearli garment
wonder sort white sarcenet embroid silver
pattern lili flower also wore around breast throat chain
shine silver stud bright sparkl gem diver sort
the third parti three youth eighteen year beauti
face seem king arthur never beheld nobl
for counten white shine hair soft
silk black possibl curl upon
shoulder eye larg bright extraordinarili black
eyebrow arch smoothli paint
could mark upon forehead evenli

sidenot king arthur findeth sir pellia upon kneel

inde caus know well
affirm friend friend upon mani sever occas

now hath alreadi fulli told sir pellia book

wonder citi hidden appear enchant

but sir gawain dearest friend sir pellia

So sir ewain beheld knight sir pellia emit great
cri joy ran catch arm sir pellia

happi behold

then sir pellia came king arthur kneel kiss
hand bounden duti everi knight unto lord

Ha messir quoth king arthur methought beheld ladi
would far distant then said unto ladi
lake ladi prithe tell fair youth
for methink never beheld nobl beauti counten
mayb make us acquaint also

lord said ladi nymu qualiti shall
hope made manifest due time would wish
known even unto but touch may say

but anon see feast spread

merri togeth shall speak matter

sidenot the ladi lake prepareth feast king arthur So
six went sat tabl spread
open meadowland for night pleasant warm wonder
full moon shone upon marvel lustr
pleasant air soft warm forest score
bright waxen taper stood silver candlestick upon tabl
taper sparkl bright star night made illumin

pellia ladi toward court camelot
otherwhil sir pellia ladi told marvel thing

believ court heaven could fairer court
fairyland whenc come

then feast end ladi lake said king arthur
sir favor way certain thing would
ask To king arthur made repli ask ladi
shall grant thee matter may sir said ladi
lake would ask would ask look upon
youth sit besid He dear well
make know dear brought hither
dwellingplac one certain reason wit make
knight that great favor would ask To intent
brought armor appurten knighthood
nobl lineag armor world could good

ladi quoth king arthur ask much pleasur
glad but touch armor speak custom
provid anyon make knight armor mine choos

To ladi lake smile kindli say lord pray
let case daresay armor hath provid
youth shall altogeth worthi nobil
futur credit entir content and
king arthur altogeth satisfi

sidenot Of armor etc sir launcelot and touch armor
ancient histori speaketh matter saith
sort followeth brought
enchant court lake wise wit front came two
youth lead two white mule mule bore two chest stud
silver boss In one chest hauberk armor
iron boot these bright like silver inlaid
cunningli devis figur pure gold next came two
esquir clad white robe mount upon white hors bear
one silver shield shine helmet silver
likewis wonder inlaid figur pure gold after
came two esquir one bear sword white sheath
emboss stud silver belt whereof silver facet
gold lead white charger whose coat soft
shine silk and gear furnitur hors

prologu

there certain kingdom call lyoness king countri
hight meliadu queen thereof hight ladi elizabeth
sister king mark cornwal

In countri lyoness beauti ladi
cun wick sorceress thi ladi took great love king meliadu
exceedingli nobl appear medit continu
might bring castl near

sidenot king meliadu ride ahunt now king meliadu
famou huntsman love chase thing world
except joy took love queen ladi elizabeth So
upon certain day late autumn season mind go forth
ahunt although day cold bleak

about prime day hound start sudden
wonder stag for white horn gild bright
shine like pure gold creatur appear like live
miracl forest when stag broke cover hound immedi
set chase great outcri yell though
suddenli gone frantic king beheld creatur also
immedi seiz great furi chase for behold

pass court littl left altogeth behind
chase entir alon forest

sidenot king meliadu chase stag the stag hound close

beheld midst plain consider lake water
midst water island upon island

speed come lake leap water swam across
island thin sheet clear ice upon water close
either bank

stint pursuit stood whimper upon brink ice

immedi leap hors plung water swam

castl courtyard thereof king meliadu ran
then immedi enter gate castl shut
king meliadu prison

prologu

the father sir perciv king hight pellinor fought

arthur for fight king arthur obtain famou
sword excalibur therein told

now king pellinor one eleven king begin
king arthur reign rebellion king arthur hath

yield overcom So king arthur drove town town
place place last driven away
habit men forest like wild beast

took wilder wife four son wit
lamorack aglav dornar perciv Of perciv
three year age other except dornar nigh estat
manhood thereaft nobl famili dwelt forest like hunt
anim great hardship ladi
queen likewis greatli peril young child
perciv

now perciv extraordinarili beauti mother love
son wherefor fear lest young child die
hardship wilder

So one day king pellinor said dear love wise prepar

child shall grown year statur estat manhood
may defend

now onetim possess two left one
lone castl forest unto betak
way solitari tower great distanc
desol part world mani mountain unto
place shall send ye like mine enemi
ever find ye

So child groweth lone place
manhood weak bodi timid spirit thou shalt make
clerk holi order but groweth shall prove
strong lusti frame high spirit shall desir undertak
deed knighthood thou shalt stay desir
shall let go forth world shall mind

and time come desireth go thu world
behold ring set preciou rubi let bring

great glad

singl tower reach sky like unto finger
stone

perciv knew naught world sort grew
altogeth wild entir innoc like littl child

In mean time year happen ill hous
king pellinor for though king arthur becam reconcil king pellinor
yet king arthur court mani bitter enemi
good worthi knight So came first king pellinor slain
treacheri sir aglav sir dornar slain
way sir lamorack alon left nobl famili

and said sir gawain brother implic
murder enemi unto king pellinor great reproach hath
alway clung treacher unknightli way
nobl knight hous pellinor slain

smote hand togeth wept great passion and cri

wick murder for perish also heart would sure
break

one told live entir ignor world

could pierc bird upon wing air
